SELECT <f:l.Id> AS LedgerId, <f:tl.TaxId> AS CorrectTaxId, <f:v.VoucherId>, <f:v.VoucherNo1>
FROM <t:AcVoucherBase v>, <t:AcOiTransaction t>, <t:AcLedger l>, <t:AcTaxLink tl>
WHERE 
{<s:main v> <i:and>}
{<s:main tl> <i:and>}
{<s:main l> <i:and>}
{<s:main t> <i:and>}
<f:v.VoucherId> = <f:t.VoucherId> 
AND <f:v.FolderId> = <p:=FolderId>  
AND t.<p:=AccType> = 'S' AND t.<p:=Acc> = <f:l.Id>
AND <f:l.TaxDescId> = <f:tl.AccTaxDescId>
AND <f:l.TaxIsDisabled> = 1
AND <f:tl.ValidFrom> <<= <f:v.BookingDate>
AND <f:tl.TaxId> <<>> <f:t.TaxId>
AND datediff(d,<f:tl.ValidFrom>, <f:v.VoucherDate>) = 
(
 SELECT MIN(datediff(d,<f:tl2.ValidFrom>, <f:vb.VoucherDate>)) 
 FROM <t:AcTaxLink tl2>, <t:AcVoucherBase vb>, <t:AcOiTransaction oi>
 WHERE 
    {<s:main vb> <i:and>}
    {<s:main tl2> <i:and>}
  <f:vb.VoucherId> = <f:oi.VoucherId>  
 AND <f:vb.FolderId> = <p:=FolderId>
 AND <f:tl2.AccTaxDescId> = <f:tl2.AccTaxDescId>
 AND <f:tl2.TaxId> <<>> <f:oi.TaxId> 
 AND <f:tl2.ValidFrom> <<= <f:vb.VoucherDate>
)

>> SCI: AcSci176(DBVersion = ~, DBTypeName = MSSQL): finished parsing
SELECT l.Id AS LedgerId, tl.TaxId AS CorrectTaxId, v.VoucherId, v.VoucherNo1
FROM AcVoucherBase v, AcOiTransaction t, AcLedger l, AcTaxLink tl
WHERE 
(v.CID='01' and v.CGID='~') and
(tl.CID='01' and tl.CGID='~') and
(l.CID='01' and l.CGID='~') and
(t.CID='01' and t.CGID='~') and
v.VoucherId = t.VoucherId 
AND v.FolderId = 19196  
AND t.Acc1Type = 'S' AND t.Acc1 = l.Id
AND l.TaxDescId = tl.AccTaxDescId
AND l.TaxIsDisabled = 1
AND tl.ValidFrom <= v.BookingDate
AND tl.TaxId <> t.TaxId
AND datediff(d,tl.ValidFrom, v.VoucherDate) = 
(
 SELECT MIN(datediff(d,tl2.ValidFrom, vb.VoucherDate)) 

 FROM AcTaxLink tl2, AcVoucherBase vb, AcOiTransaction oi

 WHERE 
    (vb.CID='01' and vb.CGID='~') and
    (tl2.CID='01' and tl2.CGID='~') and
  vb.VoucherId = oi.VoucherId  
 AND vb.FolderId = 19196
 AND tl2.AccTaxDescId = tl2.AccTaxDescId
 AND tl2.TaxId <> oi.TaxId 
 AND tl2.ValidFrom <= vb.VoucherDate
)

 from AcOiTransaction c1,AcVoucherBase d1,AcBusinessEvent d2
 where (c1.CID='01' and c1.CGID='~') and (d1.CID='01' and d1.CGID='~') and c1.VoucherId=d1.VoucherId and (d2.CID='01' and d2.CGID='~') and d1.BusinessEventId=d2.BusinessEventId and d1.VoucherState<>'B' and d1.FolderId=19196 and d1.IsSplitVoucher='1' and d1.CancellationSign IN (0,4)

Parameter: TransactionId, Value: 'RSCNJBTXISRALA'
SELECT <f:e.FolderId> AS FolderId, <f:e.VoucherNo1> AS VoucherNo1, <f:c.Acc1Type> AS Acc1Type, <f:c.Acc1> AS Acc1 
FROM <t:AcOiTransaction a> 
JOIN <t:AcOiTransaction b> ON <f:a.ParentId> = <f:b.ParentId>        -- Zahlungen
JOIN <t:AcOiTransaction c> ON <f:b.ParentId> = <f:c.TransactionId>   -- Rechnung
JOIN <t:AcTaxId d> ON <f:c.TaxId> = <f:d.TaxId>                      -- Steuer auf Rechnung
JOIN <t:AcVoucherBase e> ON <f:b.VoucherId> = <f:e.VoucherId>        -- Beleg Informationen  
WHERE <f:a.TransactionId> = <p:=TransactionId> AND <f:d.DuePerPay> = 1
--Summe der Rechnung kleiner gleich Summe der Zahlungen (Überzahlung)
AND <f:c.AmountIC> << 
(
   SELECT SUM(<f:w.AmountIC>)
   FROM <t:AcOiTransaction v> 
   JOIN <t:AcOiTransaction w> ON <f:v.ParentId> = <f:w.ParentId>        -- Zahlungen
   JOIN <t:AcOiTransaction x> ON <f:w.ParentId> = <f:x.TransactionId>   -- Rechnung
   JOIN <t:AcTaxId y> ON <f:x.TaxId> = <f:y.TaxId>                      -- Steuer auf Rechnung
   JOIN <t:AcVoucherBase z> ON <f:w.VoucherId> = <f:z.VoucherId>        -- Beleg Informationen 
   WHERE <f:v.TransactionId> = <p:=TransactionId> AND <f:y.DuePerPay> = 1
)



>> SCI: AcSci1003(DBVersion = ~, DBTypeName = ~): finished parsing
SELECT e.FolderId AS FolderId, e.VoucherNo1 AS VoucherNo1, c.Acc1Type AS Acc1Type, c.Acc1 AS Acc1 
FROM AcOiTransaction a 
JOIN AcOiTransaction b ON a.ParentId = b.ParentId        -- Zahlungen
JOIN AcOiTransaction c ON b.ParentId = c.TransactionId   -- Rechnung
JOIN AcTaxId d ON c.TaxId = d.TaxId                      -- Steuer auf Rechnung
JOIN AcVoucherBase e ON b.VoucherId = e.VoucherId        -- Beleg Informationen  
WHERE a.TransactionId = 'RSCNJBTXISRALA' AND d.DuePerPay = 1
--Summe der Rechnung kleiner gleich Summe der Zahlungen (Überzahlung)
AND c.AmountIC < 
(
   SELECT SUM(w.AmountIC)
  
 FROM AcOiTransaction v 
   JOIN AcOiTransaction w ON v.ParentId = w.ParentId        -- Zahlungen
   JOIN AcOiTransaction x ON w.ParentId = x.TransactionId   -- Rechnung
   JOIN AcTaxId y ON x.TaxId = y.TaxId                      -- Steuer auf Rechnung
   JOIN AcVoucherBase z ON w.VoucherId = z.VoucherId        -- Beleg Informationen 
  
 WHERE v.TransactionId = 'RSCNJBTXISRALA' AND y.DuePerPay = 1
)
